\index{movenc.c@{movenc.c}!mov\_setup\_track\_ids@{mov\_setup\_track\_ids}}
\index{mov\_setup\_track\_ids@{mov\_setup\_track\_ids}!movenc.c@{movenc.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mov\_setup\_track\_ids()}{mov\_setup\_track\_ids()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} mov\+\_\+setup\+\_\+track\+\_\+ids (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_m_o_v_mux_context}{M\+O\+V\+Mux\+Context}} $\ast$}]{mov,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_format_context}{A\+V\+Format\+Context}} $\ast$}]{s }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Assign track ids. If option \char`\"{}use\+\_\+stream\+\_\+ids\+\_\+as\+\_\+track\+\_\+ids\char`\"{} is set, the stream ids are used as track ids.

This assumes mov-\/$>$tracks and s-\/$>$streams are in the same order and there are no gaps in either of them (so mov-\/$>$tracks\mbox{[}n\mbox{]} refers to s-\/$>$streams\mbox{[}n\mbox{]}).

As an exception, there can be more entries in s-\/$>$streams than in mov-\/$>$tracks, in which case new track ids are generated (starting after the largest found stream id).
